===============
Timegate Data Source
===============

The following section will identify all of the available Timegate Data Sources and their associated relationships with other Data Sources within Insights.

Each Data Source contains the following headings:

AbsenceRules
----------

.. list-table::
   :widths: 4 4 18 8 20 8 5 5
   :class: apitable
   :header-rows: 1

   *  - Col#
      - PK
      - Column Name
      - Join
      - Join Table/Column
      - Data Type
      - Length
      - Nulls?

   *  - 1
      - Y
      - AbsenceRuleId
      -
      - n/a
      - int
      - 10
      - NO

   *  - 2
      -
      - AbsenceRuleName
      -
      -
      - nvarchar
      - 100
      - YES

   *  - 3
      -
      - AbsenceRuleDescription
      -
      -
      - nvarchar
      - 255
      - YES

   *  - 4
      -
      - AbsenceRuleType
      -
      -
      - nvarchar
      - 50
      - YES

   *  - 5
      -
      - UnitOfMeasure
      -
      -
      - nvarchar
      - 50
      - YES

   *  - 6
      -
      - DiaryEventTypeId
      -
      - n/a
      - int
      - 10
      - YES

   *  - 7
      -
      - ModifiedDate
      -
      -
      - datetime
      - NULL
      - YES
